            function setCookieKabum(cname, cvalue) {
                document.cookie = cname + "=" + cvalue + ";path=/";
            }
            function getCookieKabum(cname) {
                var name = cname + "=";
                var decodedCookie = (document.cookie);
                var ca = decodedCookie.split(';');
                for (var i = 0; i < ca.length; i++) {
                    var c = ca[i];
                    while (c.charAt(0) == ' ') {
                        c = c.substring(1);
                    }
                    if (c.indexOf(name) == 0) {
                        return c.substring(name.length, c.length);
                    }
                }
                return "";
            }
            function sanitizeText(str) {
                if (str != null) {
                    if (str.length > 0) {
                        return str.replace(/<\/ ? [^>] +> /gi, '');
                    }
                }
            }
            function findGetParameter(parameterName) {
                var result = null,
                    tmp = [];
                location.search
                    .substr(1)
                    .split("&")
                    .forEach(function (item) {
                        tmp = item.split("=");
                        if (tmp[0] === parameterName) result = decodeURIComponent(tmp[1]);
                    });
                return result;
            }

            var utm_source = sanitizeText(findGetParameter("utm_source"));
            var utm_campaign = sanitizeText(findGetParameter("utm_campaign"));
            var utm_medium = sanitizeText(findGetParameter("utm_medium"));

            var int_banner_name = sanitizeText(findGetParameter("int_banner_name"));

            if (gclid) {

                setCookieKabum('visitor_medium', utm_medium);
            } else if (int_banner_name) {
                setCookieKabum('int_banner_name', int_banner_name);
                setCookieKabum('int_banner_creative', int_banner_creative);
                setCookieKabum('visitor_source', '', '-1');
                setCookieKabum('visitor_campaign', '', '-1');
                setCookieKabum('visitor_medium', '', '-1');
            } else if (getCookieKabum('visitor_source')) {
                setCookieKabum('visitor_source', getCookieKabum('visitor_source'));
                setCookieKabum('visitor_campaign', getCookieKabum('visitor_campaign'));
                setCookieKabum('visitor_medium', getCookieKabum('visitor_medium'));
            } else {
                setCookieKabum('visitor_source', 'direct');
                setCookieKabum('visitor_campaign', 'direct');
                setCookieKabum('visitor_medium', 'direct');
            }
        </script>

        <script src="https://static.kabum.com.br/conteudo/js/datadome/body.js"></script>

                var name = cname + "=";
                var decodedCookie = (document.cookie);
                var ca = decodedCookie.split(';');
                for (var i = 0; i < ca.length; i++) {
                    var c = ca[i];
                    while (c.charAt(0) == ' ') {
                        c = c.substring(1);
                    }
                    if (c.indexOf(name) == 0) {
                        return c.substring(name.length, c.length);
                    }
                }
                return "";
            }
            function sanitizeText(str) {
                if (str != null) {
                    if (str.length > 0) {
                        return str.replace(/<\/ ? [^>] +> /gi, '');
                    }
                }
            }
            function findGetParameter(parameterName) {
                var result = null,
                    tmp = [];
                location.search
                    .substr(1)
                    .split("&")
                    .forEach(function (item) {
                        tmp = item.split("=");
                        if (tmp[0] === parameterName) result = decodeURIComponent(tmp[1]);
                    });
                return result;
            }

            var utm_source = sanitizeText(findGetParameter("utm_source"));
            var utm_campaign = sanitizeText(findGetParameter("utm_campaign"));
            var utm_medium = sanitizeText(findGetParameter("utm_medium"));
            var gclid = sanitizeText(findGetParameter("gclid"));
            var int_banner_name = sanitizeText(findGetParameter("int_banner_name"));
            var int_banner_creative = sanitizeText(findGetParameter("int_banner_creative"));
            if (gclid) {
                setCookieKabum('visitor_source', 'google');
                setCookieKabum('visitor_campaign', 'cpc');
                setCookieKabum('visitor_medium', 'cpc');
            } else if (utm_source) {
                setCookieKabum('visitor_source', utm_source);
                setCookieKabum('visitor_campaign', utm_campaign);
                setCookieKabum('visitor_medium', utm_medium);
            } else if (int_banner_name) {
                setCookieKabum('int_banner_name', int_banner_name);
                setCookieKabum('int_banner_creative', int_banner_creative);
                setCookieKabum('visitor_source', '', '-1');
                setCookieKabum('visitor_campaign', '', '-1');
                setCookieKabum('visitor_medium', '', '-1');
            } else if (getCookieKabum('visitor_source')) {
                setCookieKabum('visitor_source', getCookieKabum('visitor_source'));
                setCookieKabum('visitor_campaign', getCookieKabum('visitor_campaign'));
                setCookieKabum('visitor_medium', getCookieKabum('visitor_medium'));
            } else {
                setCookieKabum('visitor_source', 'direct');
                setCookieKabum('visitor_campaign', 'direct');
                setCookieKabum('visitor_medium', 'direct');
            }
        </script>

        <script src="https://static.kabum.com.br/conteudo/js/datadome/body.js"></script>
       
    </body>

        <script>
            function setCookieKabum(cname, cvalue) {
                document.cookie = cname + "=" + cvalue + ";path=/";
            }
            function getCookieKabum(cname) {
                var name = cname + "=";
                var decodedCookie = (document.cookie);
                var ca = decodedCookie.split(';');
                for (var i = 0; i < ca.length; i++) {
                    var c = ca[i];
                    while (c.charAt(0) == ' ') {
                        c = c.substring(1);
                    }
                    if (c.indexOf(name) == 0) {
                        return c.substring(name.length, c.length);
                    }
                }
                return "";
            }
            function sanitizeText(str) {
                if (str != null) {
                    if (str.length > 0) {
                        return str.replace(/<\/ ? [^>] +> /gi, '');
                    }
                }
            }
            function findGetParameter(parameterName) {
                var result = null,
                    tmp = [];
                location.search
                    .substr(1)
                    .split("&")
                    .forEach(function (item) {
                        tmp = item.split("=");
                        if (tmp[0] === parameterName) result = decodeURIComponent(tmp[1]);
                    });
                return result;
            }

            var utm_source = sanitizeText(findGetParameter("utm_source"));
            var utm_campaign = sanitizeText(findGetParameter("utm_campaign"));
            var utm_medium = sanitizeText(findGetParameter("utm_medium"));
            var gclid = sanitizeText(findGetParameter("gclid"));
            var int_banner_name = sanitizeText(findGetParameter("int_banner_name"));
            var int_banner_creative = sanitizeText(findGetParameter("int_banner_creative"));
            if (gclid) {
                setCookieKabum('visitor_source', 'google');
                setCookieKabum('visitor_campaign', 'cpc');
                setCookieKabum('visitor_medium', 'cpc');
            } else if (utm_source) {
                setCookieKabum('visitor_source', utm_source);
                setCookieKabum('visitor_campaign', utm_campaign);
                setCookieKabum('visitor_medium', utm_medium);
            } else if (int_banner_name) {
                setCookieKabum('int_banner_name', int_banner_name);
                setCookieKabum('int_banner_creative', int_banner_creative);
                setCookieKabum('visitor_source', '', '-1');
                setCookieKabum('visitor_campaign', '', '-1');
                setCookieKabum('visitor_medium', '', '-1');
            } else if (getCookieKabum('visitor_source')) {
                setCookieKabum('visitor_source', getCookieKabum('visitor_source'));
                setCookieKabum('visitor_campaign', getCookieKabum('visitor_campaign'));
                setCookieKabum('visitor_medium', getCookieKabum('visitor_medium'));
            } else {
                setCookieKabum('visitor_source', 'direct');
                setCookieKabum('visitor_campaign', 'direct');
                setCookieKabum('visitor_medium', 'direct');
            }
        </script>

        <script>
            function setCookieKabum(cname, cvalue) {
                document.cookie = cname + "=" + cvalue + ";path=/";
            }
            function getCookieKabum(cname) {
                var name = cname + "=";
                var decodedCookie = (document.cookie);
                var ca = decodedCookie.split(';');
                for (var i = 0; i < ca.length; i++) {
                    var c = ca[i];
                    while (c.charAt(0) == ' ') {
                        c = c.substring(1);
                    }
                    if (c.indexOf(name) == 0) {
                        return c.substring(name.length, c.length);
                    }
                }
                return "";
            }
            function sanitizeText(str) {
                if (str != null) {
                    if (str.length > 0) {
                        return str.replace(/<\/ ? [^>] +> /gi, '');
                    }
                }
            }
            function findGetParameter(parameterName) {
                var result = null,
                    tmp = [];
                location.search
                    .substr(1)
                    .split("&")
                    .forEach(function (item) {
                        tmp = item.split("=");
                        if (tmp[0] === parameterName) result = decodeURIComponent(tmp[1]);
                    });
                return result;
            }

            var utm_source = sanitizeText(findGetParameter("utm_source"));
            var utm_campaign = sanitizeText(findGetParameter("utm_campaign"));
            var utm_medium = sanitizeText(findGetParameter("utm_medium"));
            var gclid = sanitizeText(findGetParameter("gclid"));
            var int_banner_name = sanitizeText(findGetParameter("int_banner_name"));
            var int_banner_creative = sanitizeText(findGetParameter("int_banner_creative"));
            if (gclid) {
                setCookieKabum('visitor_source', 'google');
                setCookieKabum('visitor_campaign', 'cpc');
                setCookieKabum('visitor_medium', 'cpc');
            } else if (utm_source) {
                setCookieKabum('visitor_source', utm_source);
                setCookieKabum('visitor_campaign', utm_campaign);
                setCookieKabum('visitor_medium', utm_medium);
            } else if (int_banner_name) {
                setCookieKabum('int_banner_name', int_banner_name);
                setCookieKabum('int_banner_creative', int_banner_creative);
                setCookieKabum('visitor_source', '', '-1');
                setCookieKabum('visitor_campaign', '', '-1');
                setCookieKabum('visitor_medium', '', '-1');
            } else if (getCookieKabum('visitor_source')) {
                setCookieKabum('visitor_source', getCookieKabum('visitor_source'));
                setCookieKabum('visitor_campaign', getCookieKabum('visitor_campaign'));
                setCookieKabum('visitor_medium', getCookieKabum('visitor_medium'));
            } else {
                setCookieKabum('visitor_source', 'direct');
                setCookieKabum('visitor_campaign', 'direct');
                setCookieKabum('visitor_medium', 'direct');
            }
        </script>

        <script>
            function setCookieKabum(cname, cvalue) {
                document.cookie = cname + "=" + cvalue + ";path=/";
            }
            function getCookieKabum(cname) {
                var name = cname + "=";
                var decodedCookie = (document.cookie);
                var ca = decodedCookie.split(';');
                for (var i = 0; i < ca.length; i++) {
                    var c = ca[i];
                    while (c.charAt(0) == ' ') {
                        c = c.substring(1);
                    }
                    if (c.indexOf(name) == 0) {
                        return c.substring(name.length, c.length);
                    }
                }
                return "";
            }
            function sanitizeText(str) {
                if (str != null) {
                    if (str.length > 0) {
                        return str.replace(/<\/ ? [^>] +> /gi, '');
                    }
                }
            }
            function findGetParameter(parameterName) {
                var result = null,
                    tmp = [];
                location.search
                    .substr(1)
                    .split("&")
                    .forEach(function (item) {
                        tmp = item.split("=");
                        if (tmp[0] === parameterName) result = decodeURIComponent(tmp[1]);
                    });
                return result;
            }

            var utm_source = sanitizeText(findGetParameter("utm_source"));
            var utm_campaign = sanitizeText(findGetParameter("utm_campaign"));
            var utm_medium = sanitizeText(findGetParameter("utm_medium"));
            var gclid = sanitizeText(findGetParameter("gclid"));
            var int_banner_name = sanitizeText(findGetParameter("int_banner_name"));
            var int_banner_creative = sanitizeText(findGetParameter("int_banner_creative"));
            if (gclid) {
                setCookieKabum('visitor_source', 'google');
                setCookieKabum('visitor_campaign', 'cpc');
                setCookieKabum('visitor_medium', 'cpc');
            } else if (utm_source) {
                setCookieKabum('visitor_source', utm_source);
                setCookieKabum('visitor_campaign', utm_campaign);
                setCookieKabum('visitor_medium', utm_medium);
            } else if (int_banner_name) {
                setCookieKabum('int_banner_name', int_banner_name);
                setCookieKabum('int_banner_creative', int_banner_creative);
                setCookieKabum('visitor_source', '', '-1');
                setCookieKabum('visitor_campaign', '', '-1');
                setCookieKabum('visitor_medium', '', '-1');
            } else if (getCookieKabum('visitor_source')) {
                setCookieKabum('visitor_source', getCookieKabum('visitor_source'));
                setCookieKabum('visitor_campaign', getCookieKabum('visitor_campaign'));
                setCookieKabum('visitor_medium', getCookieKabum('visitor_medium'));
            } else {
                setCookieKabum('visitor_source', 'direct');
                setCookieKabum('visitor_campaign', 'direct');
                setCookieKabum('visitor_medium', 'direct');
            }
        </script>

        <script>
            function setCookieKabum(cname, cvalue) {
                document.cookie = cname + "=" + cvalue + ";path=/";
            }
            function getCookieKabum(cname) {
                var name = cname + "=";
                var decodedCookie = (document.cookie);
                var ca = decodedCookie.split(';');
                for (var i = 0; i < ca.length; i++) {
                    var c = ca[i];
                    while (c.charAt(0) == ' ') {
                        c = c.substring(1);
                    }
                    if (c.indexOf(name) == 0) {
                        return c.substring(name.length, c.length);
                    }
                }
                return "";
            }
            function sanitizeText(str) {
                if (str != null) {
                    if (str.length > 0) {
                        return str.replace(/<\/ ? [^>] +> /gi, '');
                    }
                }
            }
            function findGetParameter(parameterName) {
                var result = null,
                    tmp = [];
                location.search
                    .substr(1)
                    .split("&")
                    .forEach(function (item) {
                        tmp = item.split("=");
                        if (tmp[0] === parameterName) result = decodeURIComponent(tmp[1]);
                    });
                return result;
            }

            var utm_source = sanitizeText(findGetParameter("utm_source"));
            var utm_campaign = sanitizeText(findGetParameter("utm_campaign"));
            var utm_medium = sanitizeText(findGetParameter("utm_medium"));
            var gclid = sanitizeText(findGetParameter("gclid"));
            var int_banner_name = sanitizeText(findGetParameter("int_banner_name"));
            var int_banner_creative = sanitizeText(findGetParameter("int_banner_creative"));
            if (gclid) {
                setCookieKabum('visitor_source', 'google');
                setCookieKabum('visitor_campaign', 'cpc');
                setCookieKabum('visitor_medium', 'cpc');
            } else if (utm_source) {
                setCookieKabum('visitor_source', utm_source);
                setCookieKabum('visitor_campaign', utm_campaign);
                setCookieKabum('visitor_medium', utm_medium);
            } else if (int_banner_name) {
                setCookieKabum('int_banner_name', int_banner_name);
                setCookieKabum('int_banner_creative', int_banner_creative);
                setCookieKabum('visitor_source', '', '-1');
                setCookieKabum('visitor_campaign', '', '-1');
                setCookieKabum('visitor_medium', '', '-1');
            } else if (getCookieKabum('visitor_source')) {
                setCookieKabum('visitor_source', getCookieKabum('visitor_source'));
                setCookieKabum('visitor_campaign', getCookieKabum('visitor_campaign'));
                setCookieKabum('visitor_medium', getCookieKabum('visitor_medium'));
            } else {
                setCookieKabum('visitor_source', 'direct');
                setCookieKabum('visitor_campaign', 'direct');
                setCookieKabum('visitor_medium', 'direct');
            }
        </script>

        <script>
            function setCookieKabum(cname, cvalue) {
                document.cookie = cname + "=" + cvalue + ";path=/";
            }
            function getCookieKabum(cname) {
                var name = cname + "=";
                var decodedCookie = (document.cookie);
                var ca = decodedCookie.split(';');
                for (var i = 0; i < ca.length; i++) {
                    var c = ca[i];
                    while (c.charAt(0) == ' ') {
                        c = c.substring(1);
                    }
                    if (c.indexOf(name) == 0) {
                        return c.substring(name.length, c.length);
                    }
                }
                return "";
            }
            function sanitizeText(str) {
                if (str != null) {
                    if (str.length > 0) {
                        return str.replace(/<\/ ? [^>] +> /gi, '');
                    }
                }
            }
            function findGetParameter(parameterName) {
                var result = null,
                    tmp = [];
                location.search
                    .substr(1)
                    .split("&")
                    .forEach(function (item) {
                        tmp = item.split("=");
                        if (tmp[0] === parameterName) result = decodeURIComponent(tmp[1]);
                    });
                return result;
            }

            var utm_source = sanitizeText(findGetParameter("utm_source"));
            var utm_campaign = sanitizeText(findGetParameter("utm_campaign"));
            var utm_medium = sanitizeText(findGetParameter("utm_medium"));
            var gclid = sanitizeText(findGetParameter("gclid"));
            var int_banner_name = sanitizeText(findGetParameter("int_banner_name"));
            var int_banner_creative = sanitizeText(findGetParameter("int_banner_creative"));
            if (gclid) {
                setCookieKabum('visitor_source', 'google');
                setCookieKabum('visitor_campaign', 'cpc');
                setCookieKabum('visitor_medium', 'cpc');
            } else if (utm_source) {
                setCookieKabum('visitor_source', utm_source);
                setCookieKabum('visitor_campaign', utm_campaign);
                setCookieKabum('visitor_medium', utm_medium);
            } else if (int_banner_name) {
                setCookieKabum('int_banner_name', int_banner_name);
                setCookieKabum('int_banner_creative', int_banner_creative);
                setCookieKabum('visitor_source', '', '-1');
                setCookieKabum('visitor_campaign', '', '-1');
                setCookieKabum('visitor_medium', '', '-1');
            } else if (getCookieKabum('visitor_source')) {
                setCookieKabum('visitor_source', getCookieKabum('visitor_source'));
                setCookieKabum('visitor_campaign', getCookieKabum('visitor_campaign'));
                setCookieKabum('visitor_medium', getCookieKabum('visitor_medium'));
            } else {
                setCookieKabum('visitor_source', 'direct');
                setCookieKabum('visitor_campaign', 'direct');
                setCookieKabum('visitor_medium', 'direct');
            }
        </script>

            function setCookieKabum(cname, cvalue) {
                document.cookie = cname + "=" + cvalue + ";path=/";
            }
            function getCookieKabum(cname) {
                var name = cname + "=";
                var decodedCookie = (document.cookie);
                var ca = decodedCookie.split(';');
                for (var i = 0; i < ca.length; i++) {
                    var c = ca[i];
                    while (c.charAt(0) == ' ') {
                        c = c.substring(1);
                    }
                    if (c.indexOf(name) == 0) {
                        return c.substring(name.length, c.length);
                    }
                }
                return "";
            }
            function sanitizeText(str) {
                if (str != null) {
                    if (str.length > 0) {
                        return str.replace(/<\/ ? [^>] +> /gi, '');
                    }
                }
            }
            function findGetParameter(parameterName) {
                var result = null,
                    tmp = [];
                location.search
                    .substr(1)
                    .split("&")
                    .forEach(function (item) {
                        tmp = item.split("=");
                        if (tmp[0] === parameterName) result = decodeURIComponent(tmp[1]);
                    });
                return result;
            }

            var utm_source = sanitizeText(findGetParameter("utm_source"));
            var utm_campaign = sanitizeText(findGetParameter("utm_campaign"));
            var utm_medium = sanitizeText(findGetParameter("utm_medium"));
            var gclid = sanitizeText(findGetParameter("gclid"));
            var int_banner_name = sanitizeText(findGetParameter("int_banner_name"));
            var int_banner_creative = sanitizeText(findGetParameter("int_banner_creative"));
            if (gclid) {
                setCookieKabum('visitor_source', 'google');
                setCookieKabum('visitor_campaign', 'cpc');
                setCookieKabum('visitor_medium', 'cpc');
            } else if (utm_source) {
                setCookieKabum('visitor_source', utm_source);
                setCookieKabum('visitor_campaign', utm_campaign);
                setCookieKabum('visitor_medium', utm_medium);
            } else if (int_banner_name) {
                setCookieKabum('int_banner_name', int_banner_name);
                setCookieKabum('int_banner_creative', int_banner_creative);
                setCookieKabum('visitor_source', '', '-1');
                setCookieKabum('visitor_campaign', '', '-1');
                setCookieKabum('visitor_medium', '', '-1');
            } else if (getCookieKabum('visitor_source')) {
                setCookieKabum('visitor_source', getCookieKabum('visitor_source'));
                setCookieKabum('visitor_campaign', getCookieKabum('visitor_campaign'));
                setCookieKabum('visitor_medium', getCookieKabum('visitor_medium'));
            } else {
                setCookieKabum('visitor_source', 'direct');
                setCookieKabum('visitor_campaign', 'direct');
                setCookieKabum('visitor_medium', 'direct');
            }
